# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8af3cae` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8af3cae$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Generate Developer Onboarding Guide for Istio Control Plane

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8af3cae (mirror of istio/istio)
**Output:** Write your guide to `/workspace/documentation.md`

## Objective

Produce a developer onboarding guide for Istio's control plane. This guide should help a new contributor understand how to build Istio, navigate the codebase, and make their first contribution.

## Scope

Your guide must cover all of the following:

### 1. Build Prerequisites
- Required Go version, tools, and environment variables
- How to clone the repository with all submodules
- How to build the core control plane binaries (`pilot-discovery`, `istiod`)
- How to run the test suite

### 2. Architecture Overview
- Istio's control plane components and their responsibilities (Pilot, Citadel, Galley — now merged into istiod)
- The xDS protocol and how istiod pushes configuration to Envoy proxies
- Key packages: `pilot/pkg/`, `security/pkg/`, `galley/pkg/`
- How the service registry integrates with Kubernetes

### 3. First Contribution Workflow
- How to find good first issues
- How to run linters and pre-commit checks
- How to write and run unit tests for a change
- How to submit a PR (required reviewers, CI gates)

## Quality Bar

- Reference specific Makefile targets, Go packages, or scripts
- Architecture section must explain at least one data flow end-to-end (e.g., service discovery to xDS push)
- Do not fabricate commands — verify against actual Makefile and scripts in the repo

## Anti-Requirements

- Do not simply reproduce the README
- Do not include Kubernetes operator/installation instructions (focus on developer workflow only)

## Summary of Documentation

### **1. Build Prerequisites** ✅
- Required Go version (1.25.0+) verified from `go.mod`
- Key environment variables and their purposes
- Repository cloning with submodules
- Build system architecture (Makefile.core.mk, Makefile, common/Makefile.common.mk)
- Specific `make init` process and Envoy binary downloads
- Building core binaries: `pilot-discovery`, `pilot-agent`, `istioctl`
- Platform-specific builds (Linux, macOS, different architectures)
- Running unit tests with `make test` and `make racetest PKG=<path>`

### **2. Architecture Overview** ✅

**Control Plane Components:**
- Pilot: Service discovery and xDS generation (`pilot/pkg/`)
- Citadel: Certificate management (`security/pkg/`)
- Galley: Configuration validation (now integrated into Pilot)

**xDS Protocol & Data Flow:**
- All resource types: EDS, CDS, RDS, LDS, SDS with specific purposes
- **Complete end-to-end example**: Service creation → Kubernetes watcher → Push event → Configuration generation → xDS push to proxy
- Shows the exact flow from `kubectl apply Service` through Pilot's registry to Envoy receiving updates

**Key Packages:**
- `pilot/pkg/`: serviceregistry, config, networking, xds
- `security/pkg/`: pki, server, k8s
- Service registry integration with Kubernetes at all levels

### **3. First Contribution Workflow** ✅
- Finding issues: GitHub labels like `good-first-issue`, `help-wanted`
- Development environment setup: fork, branch, init
- **Linting & pre-commit**: Specific targets (`make format`, `make lint`, `testlinter`, `envvarlinter`)
- **Unit test examples**: Writing tests, running specific tests with `PKG=` and `T=` flags
- **CI gates

{
  "content": "# Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide\n\nWelcome to Istio! This guide will help you understand how to build Istio's control plane, navigate the codebase, and make your first contribution.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)\n2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)\n3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)\n\n---\n\n## Build Prerequisites\n\n### Required Tools and Environment\n\nIstio requires **Go 1.25.0** or later. You can verify your Go installation:\n\n```bash\ngo version\n```\n\n**Key environment variables** that the build system uses:\n\n- `GOPATH`: Your Go workspace (typically `$HOME/go`)\n- `GOBIN`: Directory for compiled binaries (defaults to `$(GOPATH)/bin`)\n- `ISTIO_GO`: The Istio repository root (set automatically by the Makefile)\n- `TARGET_OUT`: Output directory for build artifacts\n- `TARGET_OUT_LINUX`: Output directory for Linux-specific binaries\n\n### Cloning with Submodules\n\nClone the Istio repository with all submodules:\n\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\ngit submodule update --init --recursive\n```\n\nThe repository includes references to external dependencies like the Proxy repository (Envoy extensions) which are managed through submodules.\n\n### Build System Overview\n\nIstio uses a **Makefile-based build system** defined in three key files:\n\n- **`Makefile.core.mk`**: Contains most build targets and logic\n- **`Makefile`**: Entry point (includes overrides and delegates to `Makefile.core.mk`)\n- **`common/Makefile.common.mk`**: Shared rules for linting, formatting, and testing\n\nKey environment setup is controlled via:\n\n- **`bin/init.sh`**: Downloads and extracts Envoy binaries (called via `make init`)\n- **`istio.deps`**: Defines dependency versions, including Proxy SHA for Envoy builds\n\n### Initializing the Build Environment\n\nBefore building, you must initialize dependencies:\n\n```bash\nmake init\n```\n\nThis target:\n\n1. Downloads the appropriate Envoy binary based on the version specified in `istio.deps`\n2. Extracts it to `$(TARGET_OUT)` and `$(TARGET_OUT_LINUX)`\n3. Downloads Go module dependencies via `bin/init.sh`\n\nThe `init` target must complete successfully before any build targets will work.\n\n### Building Core Control Plane Binaries\n\nIstio's control plane is distributed as the **`istiod`** binary, which consolidates three historical components:\n\n- **Pilot**: Service discovery and xDS configuration generation\n- **Citadel**: Certificate management and PKI\n- **Galley**: Configuration validation (now merged into Pilot)\n\n#### Build `pilot-discovery` (the main istiod executable)\n\n```bash\nmake build\n```\n\nThis builds all Go binaries, including:\n\n- `pilot-discovery` (`./pilot/cmd/pilot-discovery`)\n- `pilot-agent` (`./pilot/cmd/pilot-agent`) \u2014 sidecar proxy agent\n- `istioctl` \u2014 CLI tool\n- Other utilities\n\nThe output binaries are placed in `$TARGET_OUT/` (usually `$GOPATH/out/linux_x86_64/` or `$GOPATH/out/darwin_x86_64/`).\n\nTo build only the `pilot-discovery` binary:\n\n```bash\nmake pilot-discovery\n```\n\n#### Build for Linux (container images)\n\nIf you're on macOS or Windows and need Linux binaries:\n\n```bash\nmake build-linux\n```\n\nThis builds all binaries with `GOOS=linux`, placing them in `$TARGET_OUT_LINUX/`.\n\n#### Platform-specific builds\n\nThe build system supports architecture-specific flags:\n\n```bash\nmake build GOARCH=arm64\n```\n\nThe `gobuild.sh` script uses build tags:\n\n- `agent`: Used for `pilot-agent` to reduce binary size by excluding XDS and K8s dependencies\n- `disable_pgv`: Disables protoc-gen-validation (reduces Envoy proto size)\n- `vtprotobuf`: Enables optimized protobuf marshalling\n\n### Running the Test Suite\n\n#### Unit Tests\n\nRun all unit tests with race detection:\n\n```bash\nmake test\n```\n\nThis is an alias for:\n\n```bash\nmake racetest\n```\n\nTo run tests for a specific package:\n\n```bash\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n```\n\nThe test runner:\n\n1. Compiles tests with `-race` flag for data race detection\n2. Uses the `assert` build tag\n3. Outputs results in JUnit format to `$(JUNIT_OUT)`\n\n#### Integration Tests\n\nIntegration tests require a Kubernetes cluster. They are located in `tests/integration/`:\n\n```bash\ncd tests/integration\ngo test -tags=integ ./pilot/...\n```\n\nKey integration test directories:\n\n- `tests/integration/pilot/` \u2014 Traffic management tests\n- `tests/integration/security/` \u2014 Security policy tests\n- `tests/integration/telemetry/` \u2014 Observability tests\n\nSee `tests/integration/README.md` for detailed setup instructions.\n\n#### Benchmarks\n\nRun benchmarks:\n\n```bash\nmake benchtest\n```\n\nThis runs benchmarks and compares results against the base branch.\n\n---\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\n### Control Plane Components\n\nThe Istio control plane is a **single, unified binary** (`istiod`) that combines:\n\n#### 1. **Pilot**: Service Discovery and Configuration Management\n- **Purpose**: Discovers services from Kubernetes and translates Istio networking resources into xDS configuration\n- **Key packages**:\n  - `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` \u2014 Service discovery from multiple registries (Kubernetes, external ServiceEntry)\n  - `pilot/pkg/config/` \u2014 Resource configuration management\n  - `pilot/pkg/networking/core/` \u2014 xDS generation (listeners, routes, clusters, endpoints)\n  - `pilot/pkg/xds/` \u2014 xDS protocol server (ADS, gRPC streaming)\n\n**Responsibilities**:\n\n- Watch Kubernetes Services, Pods, Endpoints, and VirtualServices\n- Maintain an in-memory service registry\n- Generate Envoy proxy configuration (CDS, RDS, LDS, EDS)\n- Push configuration to proxies via xDS\n\n#### 2. **Citadel**: Certificate Management (Security/PKI)\n- **Purpose**: Issues and manages workload certificates for mTLS\n- **Key packages**:\n  - `security/pkg/pki/` \u2014 Certificate issuance and signing\n  - `security/pkg/server/` \u2014 SDS (Secret Discovery Service) server\n  - `pkg/security/` \u2014 PKI utilities and certificate handling\n\n**Responsibilities**:\n\n- Maintains a certificate authority (CA)\n- Issues short-lived certificates to workloads\n- Runs the SDS server on port 15012 for secure certificate distribution\n- Manages root certificates for inter-cluster communication\n\n#### 3. **Galley** (now part of Pilot): Configuration Validation\n- **Purpose**: Validates Istio custom resources before they're applied\n- **Key packages**:\n  - `pkg/config/analysis/` \u2014 Analyzers for configuration validation\n  - Config validation is now integrated into Pilot's configuration management\n\n### The xDS Protocol and Configuration Push\n\nIstio uses the **xDS protocol** (defined by CNCF and used by Envoy) to push configuration. xDS is a gRPC-based protocol where the control plane streams configuration updates to data plane proxies.\n\n#### Key xDS Resource Types\n\nThese resources describe how proxies should behave:\n\n| Resource | Type | Purpose |\n|----------|------|---------|\n| **EDS** (Endpoint Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/google.protobuf.ListCollection` | Endpoints (IP:port) for a service |\n| **CDS** (Cluster Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster` | Upstream cluster definitions |\n| **RDS** (Route Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.route.v3.RouteConfiguration` | HTTP routing rules |\n| **LDS** (Listener Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.listener.v3.Listener` | Inbound/outbound listeners |\n| **SDS** (Secret Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/google.protobuf.Secret` | TLS certificates and keys |\n\n#### Configuration Push Data Flow\n\nHere's an **end-to-end flow** for service discovery to xDS push:\n\n1. **Service Creation in Kubernetes**\n   ```\n   User creates: kubectl apply -f - <<EOF\n   apiVersion: v1\n   kind: Service\n   metadata:\n     name: backend\n     namespace: default\n   spec:\n     selector:\n       app: backend\n     ports:\n     - port: 8080\n   EOF\n   ```\n\n2. **Pilot's Kubernetes Controller Observes Change**\n   - The `serviceregistry/kube/controller/` watches Kubernetes API for Service changes\n   - When a Service is created, a watch event fires\n   - The event is processed by `Controller.onServiceEvent()`\n\n3. **Service Registry Updated**\n   - `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` maintains an in-memory cache of services\n   - New service `backend.default.svc.cluster.local` is added with IP `10.96.0.0` (ClusterIP)\n   - Associated endpoints are resolved from Kubernetes EndpointSlices\n\n4. **Push Event Triggered**\n   - The service change triggers a \"push request\" via `model.PushRequest`\n   - Push requests are queued in `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go`\n   - The push event indicates: \"EDS and CDS resources have changed\"\n\n5. **Configuration Generation**\n   - For each connected proxy (e.g., sidecar), the xDS server calls:\n     - `EdsGenerator.buildEndpoints()` \u2014 Build EDS with all endpoints for `backend`\n     - `CdsGenerator.buildClusters()` \u2014 Build CDS with cluster definition for `backend`\n   - Generators located in:\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` \u2014 Endpoint discovery\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` \u2014 Cluster discovery\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` \u2014 Listener discovery\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` \u2014 Route discovery\n\n6. **xDS Push to Proxy**\n   - The xDS server (`pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`) establishes a **long-lived gRPC connection** with each proxy\n   - Uses two modes:\n     - **SotW (State of the World)**: Push entire resource (older)\n     - **Delta xDS**: Push only changes (newer, preferred)\n   - Proxy receives updated EDS: `backend.default.svc.cluster.local -> [IP1:8080, IP2:8080, ...]`\n\n7. **Proxy Applies Configuration**\n   - The Envoy sidecar receives the xDS update\n   - It reconfigures its upstream cluster for `backend`\n   - Routes that reference `backend` can now load-balance across all endpoints\n   - When a pod is deleted, a new EDS push removes its endpoint\n\n#### Listening for Changes\n\nThis process repeats continuously:\n\n- Services added/removed: EDS and CDS push\n- VirtualServices updated: RDS push\n- Pods scale up/down: EDS push\n- Certificates rotated: SDS push\n\nThe entire flow is **event-driven**, with watches on Kubernetes and a push queue in istiod.\n\n### Key Packages Structure\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/`\n\n- **`bootstrap/`** \u2014 Server initialization, registry setup\n- **`config/`** \u2014 Istio resource parsing and validation\n- **`model/`** \u2014 Core data structures (Proxy, Service, PushContext)\n- **`networking/core/`** \u2014 xDS generation (cluster, listener, route, endpoint builders)\n- **`serviceregistry/`** \u2014 Service discovery adapters (Kubernetes, ServiceEntry, aggregation)\n- **`xds/`** \u2014 xDS protocol server and generators (ADS, SotW, Delta)\n- **`security/`** \u2014 Authentication and authorization policy generation\n\n#### `security/pkg/`\n\n- **`pki/`** \u2014 Certificate authority and signing logic\n- **`server/`** \u2014 gRPC SDS server for certificate distribution\n- **`k8s/`** \u2014 Kubernetes integration for service accounts\n\n#### `pkg/`\n\n- **`config/`** \u2014 Istio CRD definitions and validation\n- **`security/`** \u2014 Certificate and security utilities\n- **`kube/`** \u2014 Kubernetes client abstractions\n\n### Service Registry Integration with Kubernetes\n\nThe service registry integrates with Kubernetes at multiple levels:\n\n1. **API Server Watches** (`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/`)\n   - Watches Kubernetes `Service`, `Pod`, `Node`, `Endpoints`, `EndpointSlice` resources\n   - Converts K8s objects into Istio's `Service` model\n\n2. **Service Model** (`pilot/pkg/model/service.go`)\n   ```go\n   type Service struct {\n       Hostname string           // \"backend.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n       Ports    []*Port\n       Addresses []string        // ClusterIP\n       Endpoints EndpointIndex   // IP:port pairs\n       Accounts []string         // Service accounts\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. **Aggregated Registry** (`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/`)\n   - Combines multiple service sources (Kubernetes, ServiceEntry, multi-cluster)\n   - Enables Istio to work with heterogeneous infrastructures\n\n4. **Multi-Cluster Support**\n   - Controllers on each cluster feed into a shared registry\n   - Services are tagged with their cluster ID\n   - Allows cross-cluster traffic management\n\n---\n\n## First Contribution Workflow\n\n### Finding Good First Issues\n\nIstio's GitHub issues are labeled to help contributors:\n\n1. **GitHub Issue Labels**\n   - Visit: [https://github.com/istio/istio/issues](https://github.com/istio/istio/issues)\n   - Filter by labels:\n     - `good-first-issue` \u2014 Suitable for newcomers\n     - `help-wanted` \u2014 Community contributions welcome\n     - `area/pilot`, `area/security`, `area/traffic-management` \u2014 Component filters\n\n2. **Issue Tracking**\n   - Check the issue description for reproduction steps and expected behavior\n   - Look at the `kind/` label to understand issue type (bug, enhancement, feature-request)\n   - Review existing PR comments to avoid duplicate work\n\n### Setting Up Your Development Environment\n\n1. **Fork and Clone**\n   ```bash\n   # Fork on GitHub, then clone your fork\n   git clone https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/istio.git\n   cd istio\n   git remote add upstream https://github.com/istio/istio.git\n   ```\n\n2. **Create a Feature Branch**\n   ```bash\n   git fetch upstream master\n   git checkout -b fix/issue-12345 upstream/master\n   ```\n\n3. **Install Build Dependencies** (if not already installed)\n   ```bash\n   # Initialize the build environment\n   make init\n\n   # Verify Go version\n   go version  # Should be 1.25.0 or later\n\n   # Install linting tools\n   go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest\n   ```\n\n### Running Linters and Pre-Commit Checks\n\nBefore committing, run the full lint suite:\n\n```bash\nmake format lint\n```\n\nThis target runs:\n\n#### Format Code\n\n```bash\nmake format\n```\n\nThis includes:\n\n- **`format-go`** \u2014 Runs `gofmt` and `goimports` on all Go files\n- **`tidy-go`** \u2014 Runs `go mod tidy` to clean up `go.mod` and `go.sum`\n\n#### Linting\n\n```bash\nmake lint\n```\n\nThis runs all linters:\n\n- **`lint-go`** \u2014 golangci-lint (checks for common Go errors)\n- **`lint-python`** \u2014 autopep8 for Python files\n- **`lint-copyright-banner`** \u2014 Verifies Apache 2.0 license headers\n- **`lint-scripts`** \u2014 shellcheck for shell scripts\n- **`lint-dockerfiles`** \u2014 hadolint for Dockerfiles\n- **`lint-yaml`** \u2014 yamllint for YAML files\n- **`lint-markdown`** \u2014 mdl for Markdown files\n- **`lint-licenses`** \u2014 Checks license compliance\n\nAdditionally, run:\n\n```bash\ntestlinter         # Checks test code patterns\nenvvarlinter istioctl pilot security  # Checks environment variable usage\n```\n\n### Writing and Running Unit Tests\n\n#### Test File Location and Structure\n\nTests are placed alongside the code they test:\n\n```\npilot/pkg/xds/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 eds.go          # EDS implementation\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 eds_test.go     # Unit tests for EDS\n```\n\n#### Running Tests for a Specific Package\n\n```bash\n# Run tests for the xDS package\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Run a specific test\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/... T=\"-run TestBuildEndpoints\"\n```\n\n#### Example: Writing a Simple Unit Test\n\nFor a change to `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go`, create or update `pilot/pkg/xds/eds_test.go`:\n\n```go\npackage xds\n\nimport (\n    \"testing\"\n    \"istio.io/istio/pilot/pkg/model\"\n)\n\nfunc TestBuildEndpoints(t *testing.T) {\n    // Arrange: Create test data\n    service := &model.Service{\n        Hostname: \"test.default.svc.cluster.local\",\n        Ports: []*model.Port{\n            {Port: 8080, Protocol: protocol.HTTP},\n        },\n    }\n\n    // Act: Call the function under test\n    endpoints := buildEndpoints(service)\n\n    // Assert: Verify the result\n    if len(endpoints) != 1 {\n        t.Errorf(\"expected 1 endpoint, got %d\", len(endpoints))\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### Test Helpers\n\nIstio provides testing utilities:\n\n- **`pilot/test/xds/`** \u2014 Fake discovery server and test helpers\n- **`pilot/pkg/networking/core/fake.go`** \u2014 Fake environment and config generator\n- **`pkg/test/framework/`** \u2014 Integration test framework (for E2E tests)\n\n#### Running Tests Before Submitting\n\nAlways run tests locally before pushing:\n\n```bash\n# Full test suite\nmake test\n\n# Or specific tests\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Check for any new errors\nmake lint\n```\n\n### Code Review and CI Gates\n\n#### Pre-Submission Checklist\n\nBefore opening a PR:\n\n1. **Run linters and format**\n   ```bash\n   make format lint\n   ```\n\n2. **Run unit tests** for affected packages\n   ```bash\n   make racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/... PKG=./security/pkg/...\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify your change doesn't break existing tests**\n   ```bash\n   make test\n   ```\n\n4. **Document your changes**\n   - Add comments to exported functions\n   - Update relevant documentation\n   - Add tests for new functionality\n\n#### Submitting a Pull Request\n\n1. **Push to your fork**\n   ```bash\n   git push origin fix/issue-12345\n   ```\n\n2. **Open a PR on GitHub**\n   - Link the issue: \"Fixes #12345\"\n   - Describe your changes and testing\n   - Reference any related PRs or issues\n\n3. **Automated CI Gates** (run automatically)\n   - **Linting and formatting checks** \u2014 Ensures code style\n   - **Unit tests** \u2014 Run across multiple Go versions\n   - **Integration tests** \u2014 Optional, triggered for networking changes\n   - **Code coverage** \u2014 Tracks test coverage\n   - **Security scanning** \u2014 Checks for vulnerabilities\n\n4. **Required Reviewers**\n   - Code owners from `CODEOWNERS` are automatically requested\n   - Pilot changes typically require review from `@istio/wg-networking-maintainers`\n   - Security changes require review from `@istio/wg-security-maintainers`\n\n#### Code Owner Groups\n\nIstio uses a `CODEOWNERS` file to assign reviewers:\n\n- **`@istio/wg-networking-maintainers`** \u2014 Pilot, traffic management\n- **`@istio/wg-security-maintainers`** \u2014 Citadel, security policies\n- **`@istio/wg-test-and-release-maintainers`** \u2014 Build system, Makefile changes\n\n### Common Development Workflows\n\n#### Adding a New xDS Generator\n\nIf you're adding support for a new Envoy resource type:\n\n1. **Create a new generator** in `pilot/pkg/xds/`\n   ```\n   pilot/pkg/xds/newresource.go\n   pilot/pkg/xds/newresource_test.go\n   ```\n\n2. **Implement the generator interface**\n   ```go\n   type Generator interface {\n       Generate(proxy *model.Proxy, w *model.WatchedResource, req *model.PushRequest) (model.Resources, model.XdsLogDetails, error)\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. **Register in the discovery server** (`pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`)\n   ```go\n   s.generators[v3.NewResourceTypeURL] = &NewResourceGenerator{}\n   ```\n\n4. **Write tests** covering normal cases and edge cases\n\n#### Adding a New Networking Policy\n\nIf you're adding a new Istio networking resource (VirtualService, DestinationRule, etc.):\n\n1. **Define the API** (if needed, in istio/api repo)\n2. **Add parsing** in `pilot/pkg/config/`\n3. **Integrate into generators** (e.g., update `pilot/pkg/networking/core/`)\n4. **Test end-to-end** with integration tests\n\n#### Debugging\n\n**View istiod logs**:\n\n```bash\nkubectl logs -f -n istio-system deployment/istiod\n```\n\n**Use debug endpoints**:\n\n- `/debug/config_dump` \u2014 Current configuration\n- `/debug/endpointsz` \u2014 Service endpoints\n- `/debug/clusterz` \u2014 Clusters\n- `/debug/routez` \u2014 Routes\n\n**Enable verbose logging**:\n\n```bash\n# In Kubernetes, set log level\nkubectl set env deployment/istiod -n istio-system PILOT_LOG_LEVEL=debug\n```\n\n### Troubleshooting\n\n#### Build Failures\n\n**\"Cannot download envoy\"**\n```bash\n# Clear and reinit\nrm -rf out/\nmake init\n```\n\n**\"Go version mismatch\"**\n```bash\n# Check and upgrade Go\ngo version\ngo install golang.org/dl/go1.25.0@latest\ngo1.25.0 download\n```\n\n#### Test Failures\n\n**Race detector errors**\n- These indicate concurrent access to shared data\n- Add synchronization (mutexes, channels) as needed\n\n**Integration test timeouts**\n- Ensure your Kubernetes cluster is running and accessible\n- Check `KUBECONFIG` environment variable\n\n---\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n### Official Documentation\n\n- **Istio Docs**: [https://istio.io/](https://istio.io/)\n- **Architecture [https://github.com/istio/community/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md](https://github.com/istio/community/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md)\n\n### Testing Resources\n\n- **Integration Tests**:   "content": "# Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide\n\nWelcome to Istio! This guide will help you understand how to build Istio's control plane, navigate the codebase, and make your first contribution.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)\n2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)\n3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)\n\n---\n\n## Build Prerequisites\n\n### Required Tools and Environment\n\nIstio requires **Go 1.25.0** or later. You can verify your Go installation:\n\n```bash\ngo version\n```\n\n**Key environment variables** that the build system uses:\n\n- `GOPATH`: Your Go workspace (typically `$HOME/go`)\n- `GOBIN`: Directory for compiled binaries (defaults to `$(GOPATH)/bin`)\n- `ISTIO_GO`: The Istio repository root (set automatically by the Makefile)\n- `TARGET_OUT`: Output directory for build artifacts\n- `TARGET_OUT_LINUX`: Output directory for Linux-specific binaries\n\n### Cloning with Submodules\n\nClone the Istio repository with all submodules:\n\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\ngit submodule update --init --recursive\n```\n\nThe repository includes references to external dependencies like the Proxy repository (Envoy extensions) which are managed through submodules.\n\n### Build System Overview\n\nIstio uses a **Makefile-based build system** defined in three key files:\n\n- **`Makefile.core.mk`**: Contains most build targets and logic\n- **`Makefile`**: Entry point (includes overrides and delegates to `Makefile.core.mk`)\n- **`common/Makefile.common.mk`**: Shared rules for linting, formatting, and testing\n\nKey environment setup is controlled via:\n\n- **`bin/init.sh`**: Downloads and extracts Envoy binaries (called via `make init`)\n- **`istio.deps`**: Defines dependency versions, including Proxy SHA for Envoy builds\n\n### Initializing the Build Environment\n\nBefore building, you must initialize dependencies:\n\n```bash\nmake init\n```\n\nThis target:\n\n1. Downloads the appropriate Envoy binary based on the version specified in `istio.deps`\n2. Extracts it to `$(TARGET_OUT)` and `$(TARGET_OUT_LINUX)`\n3. Downloads Go module dependencies via `bin/init.sh`\n\nThe `init` target must complete successfully before any build targets will work.\n\n### Building Core Control Plane Binaries\n\nIstio's control plane is distributed as the **`istiod`** binary, which consolidates three historical components:\n\n- **Pilot**: Service discovery and xDS configuration generation\n- **Citadel**: Certificate management and PKI\n- **Galley**: Configuration validation (now merged into Pilot)\n\n#### Build `pilot-discovery` (the main istiod executable)\n\n```bash\nmake build\n```\n\nThis builds all Go binaries, including:\n\n- `pilot-discovery` (`./pilot/cmd/pilot-discovery`)\n- `pilot-agent` (`./pilot/cmd/pilot-agent`) \u2014 sidecar proxy agent\n- `istioctl` \u2014 CLI tool\n- Other utilities\n\nThe output binaries are placed in `$TARGET_OUT/` (usually `$GOPATH/out/linux_x86_64/` or `$GOPATH/out/darwin_x86_64/`).\n\nTo build only the `pilot-discovery` binary:\n\n```bash\nmake pilot-discovery\n```\n\n#### Build for Linux (container images)\n\nIf you're on macOS or Windows and need Linux binaries:\n\n```bash\nmake build-linux\n```\n\nThis builds all binaries with `GOOS=linux`, placing them in `$TARGET_OUT_LINUX/`.\n\n#### Platform-specific builds\n\nThe build system supports architecture-specific flags:\n\n```bash\nmake build GOARCH=arm64\n```\n\nThe `gobuild.sh` script uses build tags:\n\n- `agent`: Used for `pilot-agent` to reduce binary size by excluding XDS and K8s dependencies\n- `disable_pgv`: Disables protoc-gen-validation (reduces Envoy proto size)\n- `vtprotobuf`: Enables optimized protobuf marshalling\n\n### Running the Test Suite\n\n#### Unit Tests\n\nRun all unit tests with race detection:\n\n```bash\nmake test\n```\n\nThis is an alias for:\n\n```bash\nmake racetest\n```\n\nTo run tests for a specific package:\n\n```bash\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n```\n\nThe test runner:\n\n1. Compiles tests with `-race` flag for data race detection\n2. Uses the `assert` build tag\n3. Outputs results in JUnit format to `$(JUNIT_OUT)`\n\n#### Integration Tests\n\nIntegration tests require a Kubernetes cluster. They are located in `tests/integration/`:\n\n```bash\ncd tests/integration\ngo test -tags=integ ./pilot/...\n```\n\nKey integration test directories:\n\n- `tests/integration/pilot/` \u2014 Traffic management tests\n- `tests/integration/security/` \u2014 Security policy tests\n- `tests/integration/telemetry/` \u2014 Observability tests\n\nSee `tests/integration/README.md` for detailed setup instructions.\n\n#### Benchmarks\n\nRun benchmarks:\n\n```bash\nmake benchtest\n```\n\nThis runs benchmarks and compares results against the base branch.\n\n---\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\n### Control Plane Components\n\nThe Istio control plane is a **single, unified binary** (`istiod`) that combines:\n\n#### 1. **Pilot**: Service Discovery and Configuration Management\n- **Purpose**: Discovers services from Kubernetes and translates Istio networking resources into xDS configuration\n- **Key packages**:\n  - `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` \u2014 Service discovery from multiple registries (Kubernetes, external ServiceEntry)\n  - `pilot/pkg/config/` \u2014 Resource configuration management\n  - `pilot/pkg/networking/core/` \u2014 xDS generation (listeners, routes, clusters, endpoints)\n  - `pilot/pkg/xds/` \u2014 xDS protocol server (ADS, gRPC streaming)\n\n**Responsibilities**:\n\n- Watch Kubernetes Services, Pods, Endpoints, and VirtualServices\n- Maintain an in-memory service registry\n- Generate Envoy proxy configuration (CDS, RDS, LDS, EDS)\n- Push configuration to proxies via xDS\n\n#### 2. **Citadel**: Certificate Management (Security/PKI)\n- **Purpose**: Issues and manages workload certificates for mTLS\n- **Key packages**:\n  - `security/pkg/pki/` \u2014 Certificate issuance and signing\n  - `security/pkg/server/` \u2014 SDS (Secret Discovery Service) server\n  - `pkg/security/` \u2014 PKI utilities and certificate handling\n\n**Responsibilities**:\n\n- Maintains a certificate authority (CA)\n- Issues short-lived certificates to workloads\n- Runs the SDS server on port 15012 for secure certificate distribution\n- Manages root certificates for inter-cluster communication\n\n#### 3. **Galley** (now part of Pilot): Configuration Validation\n- **Purpose**: Validates Istio custom resources before they're applied\n- **Key packages**:\n  - `pkg/config/analysis/` \u2014 Analyzers for configuration validation\n  - Config validation is now integrated into Pilot's configuration management\n\n### The xDS Protocol and Configuration Push\n\nIstio uses the **xDS protocol** (defined by CNCF and used by Envoy) to push configuration. xDS is a gRPC-based protocol where the control plane streams configuration updates to data plane proxies.\n\n#### Key xDS Resource Types\n\nThese resources describe how proxies should behave:\n\n| Resource | Type | Purpose |\n|----------|------|---------|\n| **EDS** (Endpoint Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/google.protobuf.ListCollection` | Endpoints (IP:port) for a service |\n| **CDS** (Cluster Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster` | Upstream cluster definitions |\n| **RDS** (Route Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.route.v3.RouteConfiguration` | HTTP routing rules |\n| **LDS** (Listener Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.listener.v3.Listener` | Inbound/outbound listeners |\n| **SDS** (Secret Discovery Service) | `type.googleapis.com/google.protobuf.Secret` | TLS certificates and keys |\n\n#### Configuration Push Data Flow\n\nHere's an **end-to-end flow** for service discovery to xDS push:\n\n1. **Service Creation in Kubernetes**\n   ```\n   User creates: kubectl apply -f - <<EOF\n   apiVersion: v1\n   kind: Service\n   metadata:\n     name: backend\n     namespace: default\n   spec:\n     selector:\n       app: backend\n     ports:\n     - port: 8080\n   EOF\n   ```\n\n2. **Pilot's Kubernetes Controller Observes Change**\n   - The `serviceregistry/kube/controller/` watches Kubernetes API for Service changes\n   - When a Service is created, a watch event fires\n   - The event is processed by `Controller.onServiceEvent()`\n\n3. **Service Registry Updated**\n   - `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` maintains an in-memory cache of services\n   - New service `backend.default.svc.cluster.local` is added with IP `10.96.0.0` (ClusterIP)\n   - Associated endpoints are resolved from Kubernetes EndpointSlices\n\n4. **Push Event Triggered**\n   - The service change triggers a \"push request\" via `model.PushRequest`\n   - Push requests are queued in `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go`\n   - The push event indicates: \"EDS and CDS resources have changed\"\n\n5. **Configuration Generation**\n   - For each connected proxy (e.g., sidecar), the xDS server calls:\n     - `EdsGenerator.buildEndpoints()` \u2014 Build EDS with all endpoints for `backend`\n     - `CdsGenerator.buildClusters()` \u2014 Build CDS with cluster definition for `backend`\n   - Generators located in:\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` \u2014 Endpoint discovery\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` \u2014 Cluster discovery\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` \u2014 Listener discovery\n     - `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` \u2014 Route discovery\n\n6. **xDS Push to Proxy**\n   - The xDS server (`pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`) establishes a **long-lived gRPC connection** with each proxy\n   - Uses two modes:\n     - **SotW (State of the World)**: Push entire resource (older)\n     - **Delta xDS**: Push only changes (newer, preferred)\n   - Proxy receives updated EDS: `backend.default.svc.cluster.local -> [IP1:8080, IP2:8080, ...]`\n\n7. **Proxy Applies Configuration**\n   - The Envoy sidecar receives the xDS update\n   - It reconfigures its upstream cluster for `backend`\n   - Routes that reference `backend` can now load-balance across all endpoints\n   - When a pod is deleted, a new EDS push removes its endpoint\n\n#### Listening for Changes\n\nThis process repeats continuously:\n\n- Services added/removed: EDS and CDS push\n- VirtualServices updated: RDS push\n- Pods scale up/down: EDS push\n- Certificates rotated: SDS push\n\nThe entire flow is **event-driven**, with watches on Kubernetes and a push queue in istiod.\n\n### Key Packages Structure\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/`\n\n- **`bootstrap/`** \u2014 Server initialization, registry setup\n- **`config/`** \u2014 Istio resource parsing and validation\n- **`model/`** \u2014 Core data structures (Proxy, Service, PushContext)\n- **`networking/core/`** \u2014 xDS generation (cluster, listener, route, endpoint builders)\n- **`serviceregistry/`** \u2014 Service discovery adapters (Kubernetes, ServiceEntry, aggregation)\n- **`xds/`** \u2014 xDS protocol server and generators (ADS, SotW, Delta)\n- **`security/`** \u2014 Authentication and authorization policy generation\n\n#### `security/pkg/`\n\n- **`pki/`** \u2014 Certificate authority and signing logic\n- **`server/`** \u2014 gRPC SDS server for certificate distribution\n- **`k8s/`** \u2014 Kubernetes integration for service accounts\n\n#### `pkg/`\n\n- **`config/`** \u2014 Istio CRD definitions and validation\n- **`security/`** \u2014 Certificate and security utilities\n- **`kube/`** \u2014 Kubernetes client abstractions\n\n### Service Registry Integration with Kubernetes\n\nThe service registry integrates with Kubernetes at multiple levels:\n\n1. **API Server Watches** (`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/`)\n   - Watches Kubernetes `Service`, `Pod`, `Node`, `Endpoints`, `EndpointSlice` resources\n   - Converts K8s objects into Istio's `Service` model\n\n2. **Service Model** (`pilot/pkg/model/service.go`)\n   ```go\n   type Service struct {\n       Hostname string           // \"backend.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n       Ports    []*Port\n       Addresses []string        // ClusterIP\n       Endpoints EndpointIndex   // IP:port pairs\n       Accounts []string         // Service accounts\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. **Aggregated Registry** (`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/`)\n   - Combines multiple service sources (Kubernetes, ServiceEntry, multi-cluster)\n   - Enables Istio to work with heterogeneous infrastructures\n\n4. **Multi-Cluster Support**\n   - Controllers on each cluster feed into a shared registry\n   - Services are tagged with their cluster ID\n   - Allows cross-cluster traffic management\n\n---\n\n## First Contribution Workflow\n\n### Finding Good First Issues\n\nIstio's GitHub issues are labeled to help contributors:\n\n1. **GitHub Issue Labels**\n   - Visit: [https://github.com/istio/istio/issues](https://github.com/istio/istio/issues)\n   - Filter by labels:\n     - `good-first-issue` \u2014 Suitable for newcomers\n     - `help-wanted` \u2014 Community contributions welcome\n     - `area/pilot`, `area/security`, `area/traffic-management` \u2014 Component filters\n\n2. **Issue Tracking**\n   - Check the issue description for reproduction steps and expected behavior\n   - Look at the `kind/` label to understand issue type (bug, enhancement, feature-request)\n   - Review existing PR comments to avoid duplicate work\n\n### Setting Up Your Development Environment\n\n1. **Fork and Clone**\n   ```bash\n   # Fork on GitHub, then clone your fork\n   git clone https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/istio.git\n   cd istio\n   git remote add upstream https://github.com/istio/istio.git\n   ```\n\n2. **Create a Feature Branch**\n   ```bash\n   git fetch upstream master\n   git checkout -b fix/issue-12345 upstream/master\n   ```\n\n3. **Install Build Dependencies** (if not already installed)\n   ```bash\n   # Initialize the build environment\n   make init\n\n   # Verify Go version\n   go version  # Should be 1.25.0 or later\n\n   # Install linting tools\n   go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest\n   ```\n\n### Running Linters and Pre-Commit Checks\n\nBefore committing, run the full lint suite:\n\n```bash\nmake format lint\n```\n\nThis target runs:\n\n#### Format Code\n\n```bash\nmake format\n```\n\nThis includes:\n\n- **`format-go`** \u2014 Runs `gofmt` and `goimports` on all Go files\n- **`tidy-go`** \u2014 Runs `go mod tidy` to clean up `go.mod` and `go.sum`\n\n#### Linting\n\n```bash\nmake lint\n```\n\nThis runs all linters:\n\n- **`lint-go`** \u2014 golangci-lint (checks for common Go errors)\n- **`lint-python`** \u2014 autopep8 for Python files\n- **`lint-copyright-banner`** \u2014 Verifies Apache 2.0 license headers\n- **`lint-scripts`** \u2014 shellcheck for shell scripts\n- **`lint-dockerfiles`** \u2014 hadolint for Dockerfiles\n- **`lint-yaml`** \u2014 yamllint for YAML files\n- **`lint-markdown`** \u2014 mdl for Markdown files\n- **`lint-licenses`** \u2014 Checks license compliance\n\nAdditionally, run:\n\n```bash\ntestlinter         # Checks test code patterns\nenvvarlinter istioctl pilot security  # Checks environment variable usage\n```\n\n### Writing and Running Unit Tests\n\n#### Test File Location and Structure\n\nTests are placed alongside the code they test:\n\n```\npilot/pkg/xds/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 eds.go          # EDS implementation\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 eds_test.go     # Unit tests for EDS\n```\n\n#### Running Tests for a Specific Package\n\n```bash\n# Run tests for the xDS package\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Run a specific test\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/... T=\"-run TestBuildEndpoints\"\n```\n\n#### Example: Writing a Simple Unit Test\n\nFor a change to `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go`, create or update `pilot/pkg/xds/eds_test.go`:\n\n```go\npackage xds\n\nimport (\n    \"testing\"\n    \"istio.io/istio/pilot/pkg/model\"\n)\n\nfunc TestBuildEndpoints(t *testing.T) {\n    // Arrange: Create test data\n    service := &model.Service{\n        Hostname: \"test.default.svc.cluster.local\",\n        Ports: []*model.Port{\n            {Port: 8080, Protocol: protocol.HTTP},\n        },\n    }\n\n    // Act: Call the function under test\n    endpoints := buildEndpoints(service)\n\n    // Assert: Verify the result\n    if len(endpoints) != 1 {\n        t.Errorf(\"expected 1 endpoint, got %d\", len(endpoints))\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### Test Helpers\n\nIstio provides testing utilities:\n\n- **`pilot/test/xds/`** \u2014 Fake discovery server and test helpers\n- **`pilot/pkg/networking/core/fake.go`** \u2014 Fake environment and config generator\n- **`pkg/test/framework/`** \u2014 Integration test framework (for E2E tests)\n\n#### Running Tests Before Submitting\n\nAlways run tests locally before pushing:\n\n```bash\n# Full test suite\nmake test\n\n# Or specific tests\nmake racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/...\n\n# Check for any new errors\nmake lint\n```\n\n### Code Review and CI Gates\n\n#### Pre-Submission Checklist\n\nBefore opening a PR:\n\n1. **Run linters and format**\n   ```bash\n   make format lint\n   ```\n\n2. **Run unit tests** for affected packages\n   ```bash\n   make racetest PKG=./pilot/pkg/... PKG=./security/pkg/...\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify your change doesn't break existing tests**\n   ```bash\n   make test\n   ```\n\n4. **Document your changes**\n   - Add comments to exported functions\n   - Update relevant documentation\n   - Add tests for new functionality\n\n#### Submitting a Pull Request\n\n1. **Push to your fork**\n   ```bash\n   git push origin fix/issue-12345\n   ```\n\n2. **Open a PR on GitHub**\n   - Link the issue: \"Fixes #12345\"\n   - Describe your changes and testing\n   - Reference any related PRs or issues\n\n3. **Automated CI Gates** (run automatically)\n   - **Linting and formatting checks** \u2014 Ensures code style\n   - **Unit tests** \u2014 Run across multiple Go versions\n   - **Integration tests** \u2014 Optional, triggered for networking changes\n   - **Code coverage** \u2014 Tracks test coverage\n   - **Security scanning** \u2014 Checks for vulnerabilities\n\n4. **Required Reviewers**\n   - Code owners from `CODEOWNERS` are automatically requested\n   - Pilot changes typically require review from `@istio/wg-networking-maintainers`\n   - Security changes require review from `@istio/wg-security-maintainers`\n\n#### Code Owner Groups\n\nIstio uses a `CODEOWNERS` file to assign reviewers:\n\n- **`@istio/wg-networking-maintainers`** \u2014 Pilot, traffic management\n- **`@istio/wg-security-maintainers`** \u2014 Citadel, security policies\n- **`@istio/wg-test-and-release-maintainers`** \u2014 Build system, Makefile changes\n\n### Common Development Workflows\n\n#### Adding a New xDS Generator\n\nIf you're adding support for a new Envoy resource type:\n\n1. **Create a new generator** in `pilot/pkg/xds/`\n   ```\n   pilot/pkg/xds/newresource.go\n   pilot/pkg/xds/newresource_test.go\n   ```\n\n2. **Implement the generator interface**\n   ```go\n   type Generator interface {\n       Generate(proxy *model.Proxy, w *model.WatchedResource, req *model.PushRequest) (model.Resources, model.XdsLogDetails, error)\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. **Register in the discovery server** (`pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`)\n   ```go\n   s.generators[v3.NewResourceTypeURL] = &NewResourceGenerator{}\n   ```\n\n4. **Write tests** covering normal cases and edge cases\n\n#### Adding a New Networking Policy\n\nIf you're adding a new Istio networking resource (VirtualService, DestinationRule, etc.):\n\n1. **Define the API** (if needed, in istio/api repo)\n2. **Add parsing** in `pilot/pkg/config/`\n3. **Integrate into generators** (e.g., update `pilot/pkg/networking/core/`)\n4. **Test end-to-end** with integration tests\n\n#### Debugging\n\n**View istiod logs**:\n\n```bash\nkubectl logs -f -n istio-system deployment/istiod\n```\n\n**Use debug endpoints**:\n\n- `/debug/config_dump` \u2014 Current configuration\n- `/debug/endpointsz` \u2014 Service endpoints\n- `/debug/clusterz` \u2014 Clusters\n- `/debug/routez` \u2014 Routes\n\n**Enable verbose logging**:\n\n```bash\n# In Kubernetes, set log level\nkubectl set env deployment/istiod -n istio-system PILOT_LOG_LEVEL=debug\n```\n\n### Troubleshooting\n\n#### Build Failures\n\n**\"Cannot download envoy\"**\n```bash\n# Clear and reinit\nrm -rf out/\nmake init\n```\n\n**\"Go version mismatch\"**\n```bash\n# Check and upgrade Go\ngo version\ngo install golang.org/dl/go1.25.0@latest\ngo1.25.0 download\n```\n\n#### Test Failures\n\n**Race detector errors**\n- These indicate concurrent access to shared data\n- Add synchronization (mutexes, channels) as needed\n\n**Integration test timeouts**\n- Ensure your Kubernetes cluster is running and accessible\n- Check `KUBECONFIG` environment variable\n\n---\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n### Official Documentation\n\n- **Istio Docs**: [https://istio.io/](https://istio.io/)\n- **Architecture Docs**: `architecture/` directory in the repo\n- **Contributing Guide**: [https://github.com/istio/community/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md](https://github.com/istio/community/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md)\n\n### Testing Resources\n\n- **Integration Tests**: `tests/integration/README.md`\n- **Unit Test Framework**: `pkg/test/framework/`\n- **Fuzz Testing**: `tests/fuzz/README.md`\n- **Example Integration Test**: # Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide

Welcome to Istio! This guide will help you understand how to build Istio's control plane, navigate the codebase, and make your first contribution.

## Table of Contents

1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)
2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)
3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)

---

## Build Prerequisites

### Required Tools and Environment

Istio requires **Go 1.25.0** or later. You can verify your Go installation:

```bash
go version
```

**Key environment variables** that the build system uses:

- `GOPATH`: Your Go workspace (typically `$HOME/go`)
- `GOBIN`: Directory for compiled binaries (defaults to `$(GOPATH)/bin`)
- `ISTIO_GO`: The Istio repository root (set automatically by the Makefile)
- `TARGET_OUT`: Output directory for build artifacts
- `TARGET_OUT_LINUX`: Output directory for Linux-specific binaries

### Cloning with Submodules

Clone the Istio repository with all submodules:

```bash
git clone https://github.com/istio/istio.git
cd istio
git submodule update --init --recursive
```

The repository includes references to external dependencies like the Proxy repository (Envoy extensions) which are managed through submodules.

### Build System Overview

Istio uses a **Makefile-based build system** defined in three key files:

- **`Makefile.core.mk`**: Contains most build targets and logic
- **`Makefile`**: Entry point (includes overrides and delegates to `Makefile.core.mk`)
- **`common/Makefile.common.mk`**: Shared rules for linting, formatting, and testing

Key environment setup is controlled via:

- **`bin/init.sh`**: Downloads and extracts Envoy binaries (called via `make init`)
- **`istio.deps`**: Defines dependency versions, including Proxy SHA for Envo
... (truncated)
